10.1.2
 
Integrating
 
KPIs
 
Across
 
Domains
1.
 
Financial
 
KPIs
 
○
 
Net
 
Interest
 
Margin
 
(NIM),
 
Loan-to-Deposit
 
Ratio
 
(LDR),
 
and
 
Return
 
on
 
Equity
 
(ROE)
■
 
Use
:
 
Provide
 
a
 
clear
 
view
 
of
 
proﬁtability,
 
lending
 
efficiency,
 
and
 
overall
 
ﬁnancial
 
health.
■
 
Actionable
 
Tip
:
 
If
 
NIM
 
or
 
ROE
 
dips
 
below
 
set
 
benchmarks,
 
investigate
 
whether
 
rising
 
costs,
 
inefficient
 
operations,
 
or
 
risky
 
lending
 
are
 
contributing
 
factors.
 
Develop
 
recovery
 
plans
 
(e.g.,
 
recalibrating
 
loan
 
products
 
or
 
renegotiating
 
supplier
 
contracts).
○
 
Operational
 
Efficiency
 
(Cost-to-Income
 
Ratio)
■
 
Purpose
:
 
Show
 
how
 
effectively
 
Desjardins
 
converts
 
costs
 
into
 
revenues.

■
 
Actionable
 
Tip
:
 
Identify
 
the
 
biggest
 
cost
 
drivers
 
(e.g.,
 
technology
 
investments,
 
facility
 
maintenance).
 
If
 
the
 
ratio
 
remains
 
high,
 
form
 
cross-departmental
 
task
 
forces
 
to
 
propose
 
targeted
 
improvements
 
(e.g.,
 
automation
 
of
 
manual
 
tasks,
 
renegotiation
 
of
 
vendor
 
terms).
2.
 
Operational
 
KPIs
 
○
 
Service
 
Delivery
 
Times
■
 
Focus
:
 
M easure
 
speed
 
in
 
processing
 
loans,
 
opening
 
accounts,
 
or
 
responding
 
to
 
member
 
inquiries.
■
 
Actionable
 
Tip
:
 
Set
 
a
 
baseline
 
for
 
acceptable
 
turnaround
 
(e.g.,
 
48
 
hours
 
for
 
loan
 
applications).
 
W hen
 
deviations
 
occur,
 
hold
 
short,
 
focused
 
“process
 
improvement
 
sprints”
 
to
 
diagnose
 
bottlenecks
 
and
 
implement
 
quick
 
ﬁxes.
○
 
Adoption
 
of
 
Digital
 
Platforms
■
 
Measurement
:
 
Track
 
member
 
usage
 
of
 
online
 
banking,
 
mobile
 
apps,
 
and
 
self-service
 
tools.
■
 
Actionable
 
Tip
:
 
If
 
adoption
 
lags
 
in
 
certain
 
demographics
 
(e.g.,
 
older
 
members),
 
introduce
 
targeted
 
training
 
sessions
 
or
 
simpliﬁed
 
interfaces.
 
Offer
 
incentives
 
(like
 
waived
 
fees)
 
for
 
ﬁrst-time
 
users
 
of
 
digital
 
channels.
3.
 
Non-Financial
 
KPIs
 
○
 
Leadership
 
Diversity
 
and
 
Inclusivity
■
 
Purpose
:
 
Ensure
 
decision-making
 
bodies
 
reﬂect
 
the
 
demographics
 
and
 
values
 
of
 
Desjardins’
 
membership.
■
 
Actionable
 
Tip
:
 
M andate
 
a
 
target
 
for
 
gender
 
balance
 
or
 
minority
 
representation
 
in
 
senior
 
leadership.
 
Report
 
progress
 
(e.g.,
 
percentage
 
of
 
women
 
in
 
leadership
 
roles)
 
quarterly
 
to
 
the
 
Board.
○
 
Innovation
 
Metrics
■
 
Examples
:
 
Number
 
of
 
new
 
products
 
launched,
 
pilot
 
programs
 
tested,
 
or
 
patent
 
ﬁlings
 
(if
 
applicable).
■
 
Actionable
 
Tip
:
 
Evaluate
 
adoption
 
rates
 
for
 
each
 
new
 
service,
 
collecting
 
feedback
 
on
 
user
 
experience.
 
If
 
uptake
 
is
 
slow,
 
reﬁne
 
the
 
offering
 
or
 
invest
 
in
 
more
 
member
 
education
 
before
 
expanding
 
further.
10.1.3
 
Creating
 
Actionable
 
M etrics
1.
 
Deﬁning
 
Performance
 
Thresholds
 
○
 
Acceptable,
 
Alert,
 
and
 
Critical
 
Levels
■
 
Method
:
 
Assign
 
color-coded
 
tiers
 
for
 
each
 
KPI
 
(e.g.,

for

for

■
 
Actionable
 
Tip
:
 
If

range,

with

heads,

root
 
causes
 
and

2.
 
Assigning
 
Metric
 
Ownership
 
○
 
Ownership
 
and
 
Accountability
■
 
Purpose
:
 
Designate
 
a

or

KPI,

on

and

improvements.
■
 
Actionable
 
Tip
:
 
Update
 
job
 
descriptions
 
or
 
departmental
 
objectives
 
so
 
leaders
 
clearly
 
understand
 
their
 
responsibilities
 
regarding
 
key
 
metrics
 
(e.g.,
 
“VP
 
of

owns
 
ESG

“Head
 
of

owns
 
digital
 
adoption
 
rates).
3.
 
Driving
 
Corrective

○

Monitoring
 
and

■
 
Approach
:

in

or

executive
 
and

:

“KPI

where

owners

trends,

and

when
 
needed.
By

success
 
metrics
 
beyond
 
short-term
 
ﬁnancial

and
 
integrating

into

operations,
 
Desjardins
 
stays

in

while

This

satisfaction,

and

and

leadership
 
maintain
 
strategic

continuously
 
reﬁne

experience.

M onitoring

Robust

to

in

By

have

to

10.2.1
 
Real-Time
 
Analytics
 
for
 
Insights
1.
 
Integrated
 
Monitoring
 
Platforms
 
○
 
Centralized
 
Dashboards
:
 
Consolidate
 
data
 
from
 
ﬁnancial
 
(e.g.,
 
liquidity,
 
ROE),
 
operational
 
(e.g.,
 
transaction
 
volumes),
 
and
 
member-focused
 
(e.g.,
 
satisfaction
 
scores)
 
systems
 
into
 
user-friendly
 
dashboards.
○
 
Actionable
 
Tip
:
 
Use
 
color-coded
 
heatmaps
 
or
 
trend
 
lines
 
to
 
highlight
 
underperforming
 
areas,
 
prompting
 
immediate
 
review
 
by
 
the
 
relevant
 
department
 
heads.
 
Schedule
 
automated
 
daily
 
or
 
weekly
 
reports
 
that
 
summarize
 
top
 
KPIs
 
for
 
quick
 
executive
 
review.
2.
 
Predictive
 
Analytics
 
○
 
AI-Driven
 
Forecasting
:
 
Employ
 
machine
 
learning
 
models
 
that
 
can
 
predict
 
member
 
churn
 
(e.g.,
 
likelihood
 
of
 
account
 
closures)
 
or
 
loan
 
default
 
probabilities,
 
enabling
 
preemptive
 
policy
 
adjustments.
○
 
Actionable
 
Tip
:
 
Feed
 
external
 
factors
 
(such
 
as
 
economic
 
indicators,
 
regulatory
 
changes)
 
into
 
predictive
 
models
 
to
 
reﬁne
 
accuracy.
 
If
 
churn
 
predictions
 
spike,
 
launch
 
targeted
 
retention
 
campaigns
 
(e.g.,
 
personalized
 
offers
 
or
 
outreach)
 
before
 
issues
 
escalate.
3.
 
Automated
 
Alerts
 
○
 
Threshold-Based
 
Notiﬁcations
:
 
Conﬁgure
 
system
 
alerts
 
when
 
key
 
metrics
 
breach
 
predetermined
 
“alert”
 
or
 
“critical”
 
levels
 
(e.g.,
 
liquidity
 
coverage
 
ratio
 
dipping
 
below

a

surge
 
in
 
complaints).
○
 
Actionable
 
Tip
:
 
Assign
 
each

to
 
a
 
designated
 
“owner”
 
responsible
 
for
 
triggering
 
a
 
rapid
 
response.
 
Require
 
a
 
structured
 
follow-up—like
 
a

brieﬁng—to
 
ensure
 
leadership
 
remains
 
informed
 
and
 
corrective
 
actions
 
are
 
documented.

:
 
M odel

to

ﬁnancial

:

○

and

:
